de:=1. (indicating possession; of)
>> La vosto de la kato => the cat's tail
2. of
>> Klingo de argxento => A blade of silver
>> Folio de graso => A blade of grass
3. from (indicating movement away)
>> Ni venis de Nov-Jorko => We came from New York
> See also:: el
4. by (indicating the doer of an action, when using passive style)
>> La letero skribita de la instruisto => the letter written by the teacher
